    <h4>Min Memory</h4> <span class="badge badge-success default-value">Default: null</span><br/>
    <span class="description"><p>Minimum memory allocation for dynamic memory ballooning in mebibytes (MiB). Allows VM memory to shrink     during low usage but guarantees this minimum. <code>null</code> to disable ballooning.</p>
